          - generic [ref=e325]: when the market cap is low, buy taxes decrease to encourage entry while sell taxes increase to deter early exits

          - generic [ref=e325]: when the market cap is low, buy taxes decrease to encourage entry while sell taxes increase to deter early exits

**Screenshot:** `test-results/smoke-html-structure-valid-23fae-s-has-valid-HTML5-structure-chromium/test-failed-1.png`
